# Grafana User Permission Model Role Coverage Audit

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that define and enforce the three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin): the role-to-permission mapping, the permission guard middleware, and the folder/dashboard permission inheritance.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

     1→package identity
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"fmt"
     5→	"strings"
     6→)
     7→
     8→// swagger:enum RoleType
     9→type RoleType string
    10→
    11→const (
    12→	RoleNone   RoleType = "None"
    13→	RoleViewer RoleType = "Viewer"
    14→	RoleEditor RoleType = "Editor"
    15→	RoleAdmin  RoleType = "Admin"
    16→)
    17→
    18→var rolePrecedence = map[RoleType]int{
    19→	RoleNone:   10,
    20→	RoleViewer: 20,
    21→	RoleEditor: 30,
    22→	RoleAdmin:  40,
    23→}
    24→
    25→// Needed to keep stable order
    26→var roleOrder = [...]RoleType{
    27→	RoleNone,
    28→	RoleViewer,
    29→	RoleEditor,
    30→	RoleAdmin,
    31→}
    32→
    33→func (r RoleType) IsValid() bool {
    34→	_, ok := rolePrecedence[r]
    35→	return ok
    36→}
    37→
    38→func (r RoleType) Includes(other RoleType) bool {
    39→	return rolePrecedence[r] >= rolePrecedence[other]
    40→}
    41→
    42→func (r RoleType) Children() []RoleType {
    43→	children := make([]RoleType, 0, 3)
    44→
    45→	for _, role := range roleOrder {
    46→		if rolePrecedence[r] > rolePrecedence[role] {
    47→			children = append(children, role)
    48→		}
    49→	}
    50→
    51→	return children
    52→}
    53→
    54→func (r RoleType) Parents() []RoleType {
    55→	parents := make([]RoleType, 0, 3)
    56→
    57→	for _, role := range roleOrder {
    58→		if rolePrecedence[r] < rolePrecedence[role] {

    64→}

    12→var logger = log.New("accesscontrol.evaluator")
    13→
    14→type CheckerFn func(action string, scopes ...string) (bool, error)
    15→
    16→type Evaluator interface {
    17→	// Evaluate permissions that are grouped by action
    18→	Evaluate(permissions map[string][]string) bool
    19→	// EvaluateCustom allows to perform evaluation with custom check function
    20→	EvaluateCustom(fn CheckerFn) (bool, error)
    21→	// MutateScopes executes a sequence of ScopeModifier functions on all embedded scopes of an evaluator and returns a new Evaluator
    22→	MutateScopes(ctx context.Context, mutate ScopeAttributeMutator) (Evaluator, error)
    23→	// String returns a string representation of permission required by the evaluator
    24→	fmt.Stringer
    25→	fmt.GoStringer
    26→}
    27→
    28→var _ Evaluator = new(permissionEvaluator)
    29→
    30→// EvalPermission returns an evaluator that will require at least one of passed scopes to match
    31→func EvalPermission(action string, scopes ...string) Evaluator {
    32→	return permissionEvaluator{Action: action, Scopes: scopes}
    33→}
    34→
    35→type permissionEvaluator struct {
    36→	Action string
    37→	Scopes []string
    38→}
    39→
    40→func (p permissionEvaluator) Evaluate(permissions map[string][]string) bool {
    41→	userScopes, ok := permissions[p.Action]
    42→	if !ok {
    43→		return false
    44→	}
    45→
    46→	if len(p.Scopes) == 0 {
    47→		return true
    48→	}
    49→
    50→	for _, target := range p.Scopes {
    51→		for _, scope := range userScopes {
    52→			if match(scope, targ
... (truncated)

## Grafana Three-Tier Permission Model (Viewer/Editor/Admin)

### Role-to-Permission Mapping
- **`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`** — Canonical `RoleType` definition with `RoleViewer`/`RoleEditor`/`RoleAdmin` constants and a `rolePrecedence` map that enables `Includes()` hierarchy (Admin⊃Editor⊃Viewer)
- **`pkg/services/org/model.go`** — Re-exports role constants as `org.RoleViewer`, `org.RoleEditor`, `org.RoleAdmin`
- **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`** — `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()` creates in-memory role DTOs; `DeclareFixedRoles()` wires fixed roles to org tiers
- **`pkg/api/accesscontrol.go`** — `declareFixedRoles()` assigns all HTTP API roles to Viewer/Editor/Admin grants
- **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`** — `DashboardViewActions`, `DashboardEditActions`, `DashboardAdminActions`; `registerDashboardRoles()` seeds fixed roles per tier
- **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`** — Same pattern for folders with `FolderViewActions`/`EditActions`/`AdminActions`

### Permission Guard Middleware
- **`pkg/middleware/auth.go`** — `RoleAuth()` function; `Auth()` for sign-in/Grafana-admin checks
- **`pkg/middleware/middleware.go`** — Pre-built guards: `ReqEditorRole`, `ReqOrgAdmin`, `ReqGrafanaAdmin`
- **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`** — `Middleware()` and `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()` for RBAC-based fine-grained guards; `authorize()` calls `ac.Evaluate()`
- **`pkg/services/user/identity.go`** — `SignedInUser.HasRole()` uses `OrgRole.Includes()` for hierarchical role checks

### Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance
- **`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`** — `GetInheritedScopes()` traverses ancestor folders

scope[:len(scope)-1], scope[len(scope)-1]\n\t// verify that last char is either ':' or '/' if last character of scope is '*'\n\tif len(prefix) > 0 && last == '*' {\n\t\tlastChar := prefix[len(prefix)-1]\n\t\tif lastChar != ':' && lastChar != '/' {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn !strings.ContainsAny(prefix, \"*?\")\n}\n\nfunc ManagedUserRoleName(userID int64) string folder parents: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tresult := make([]string, 0, len(ancestors))\n\tfor _, ff := range ancestors {\n\t\tresult = append(result, ScopeFoldersProvider.GetResourceScopeUID(ff.UID))\n\t}\n\n\treturn result, nil\n}\n",

three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) is defined and enforced across the following layers:\\n\\n## 1. Role Type Definition (`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`)\\n\\nThe canonical definition of `RoleType` lives in the identity package. It declares `RoleViewer`, `RoleEditor`, and `RoleAdmin` as string constants, along with a `rolePrecedence` map (None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40) that powers the `Includes()` method \u2014 making Admin include Editor which includes Viewer. The `Children()` and `Parents()` helpers derive role hierarchy from precedence. These are re-exported in `pkg/services/org/model.go` as `org.RoleViewer`, `org.RoleEditor`, `org.RoleAdmin`.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n### Basic Role Definitions (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`)\\n`BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()` creates the in-memory `RoleDTO` objects for each of the five basic roles (None, Viewer, Editor, Admin, Grafana Admin). `DeclareFixedRoles()` wires built-in fixed roles (LDAP, org users, settings, stats, users) to Grafana Admin. The `RoleRegistration.Grants` field throughout the codebase specifies which org-role tiers receive each fixed role.\\n\\n### API-level Fixed Role Grants (`pkg/api/accesscontrol.go`)\\n`HTTPServer.declareFixedRoles()` declares all the major fixed roles the HTTP API needs and assigns them to Viewer/Editor/Admin tiers. Examples: `datasourcesExplorerRole` \u2192 Editor, `datasourcesReaderRole` \u2192 Admin (or Viewer when license enforcement is off), `annotationsReaderRole` \u2192 Viewer, `annotationsWriterRole` \u2192 Editor, `dashboardsCreatorRole` \u2192 Editor, `dashboardsWriterRole` \u2192 Admin, `orgReaderRole` \u2192 Viewer, `orgWriterRole` \u2192 Admin.\\n\\n### Dashboard Permission Actions (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`)\\nDefines the three-tier action sets for dashboards:\\n- `DashboardViewActions`: `[dashboards:read]`\\n- `DashboardEditActions`: View + `[dashboards:write, dashboards:delete]`\\n- `DashboardAdminActions`: Edit + `[dashboards.permissions:read, dashboards.permissions:write]`\\n`registerDashboardRoles()` seeds `fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin` and grants them to Viewer/Editor/Admin respectively. `ProvideDashboardPermissions()` creates the resource permissions service with `PermissionsToActions` mapping View/Edit/Admin strings to action lists.\\n\\n### Folder Permission Actions (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`)\\nSimilarly defines `FolderViewActions`, `FolderEditActions`, `FolderAdminActions` (which include alerting rule and library panel actions). `registerFolderRoles()` and `ProvideFolderPermissions()` set up the equivalent three-tier action mapping for folder resources.\\n\\n### Dashboard/Folder Access Constants (`pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go`)\\nDefines the legacy `PermissionType` iota: `PERMISSION_VIEW=1`, `PERMISSION_EDIT=2`, `PERMISSION_ADMIN=4`, used in legacy ACL-based permission checks.\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n### Legacy Role Guards (`pkg/middleware/auth.go` and `pkg/middleware/middleware.go`)\\n`RoleAuth(roles ...org.RoleType)` in `auth.go` is the fundamental role-based gate: it checks `c.OrgRole == role` for any of the supplied roles and calls `accessForbidden()` if none match. `Auth(options)` handles signed-in and Grafana admin checks. In `middleware.go`, pre-built guards are exposed as package-level vars:\\n- `ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin)` \u2014 allows Editor or Admin\\n- `ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin)` \u2014 allows only Admin\\n- `ReqGrafanaAdmin` \u2014 requires server admin flag\\n\\n### RBAC Middleware (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`)\\n`Middleware(ac AccessControl)` returns a `web.Handler` factory for fine-grained RBAC guards. It calls `authorize(c, ac, user, evaluator)` which invokes `ac.Evaluate()` with scope-injected evaluators. On failure, `deny()` returns HTTP 403. `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()` handles cross-org authorization. `ReqHasRole()` in `accesscontrol.go` wraps `c.HasRole()` as an evaluator predicate.\\n\\n### AccessControl Interface and Evaluators (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go`, `evaluator.go`)\\n`AccessControl.Evaluate()` is the central permission check. `EvalPermission(action, scopes...)` creates a `permissionEvaluator` that matches the user's permission map. `EvalAll`/`EvalAny` compose evaluators.\\n\\n### Core Implementation (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/`)\\n`acimpl.AccessControl.Evaluate()` merges in-memory basic role permissions with DB-stored managed permissions. `Service.getUserPermissions()` calls `GetOrgRoles(user)` (which returns the user's role and parent roles via the precedence hierarchy) to look up basic role permissions, then fetches managed role permissions from the DB via the store.\\n\\n### User Role Resolution (`pkg/services/user/identity.go`)\\n`SignedInUser.HasRole(role)` returns true if the user is a Grafana admin OR if `u.OrgRole.Includes(role)` \u2014 i.e., the role hierarchy check. `GetOrgRole()` returns the assigned tier.\\n\\n## 4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n### Scope Resolvers (`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`)\\nPermission inheritance is implemented through scope resolution. `GetInheritedScopes()` traverses the folder tree upward via `folderSvc.GetParents()` and returns a slice of `folders:uid:<uid>` scopes for all ancestor folders. This means a permission granted on a parent folder applies to all nested folders and dashboards.\\n\\n`NewFolderUIDScopeResolver()` and `NewFolderIDScopeResolver()` convert legacy folder-id scopes into UID-based scopes, appending inherited parent scopes.\\n\\n`NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()` and `NewDashboardIDScopeResolver()` call `resolveDashboardScope()`, which looks up the dashboard's `FolderUID` and returns the dashboard scope plus the folder scope chain (via `GetInheritedScopes()`). This is how dashboard permissions inherit from their containing folders.\\n\\n### Folder Service (`pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go`, `pkg/services/folder/model.go`)\\nThe `Folder` struct stores `ParentUID` and `FullpathUIDs` for efficient ancestor traversal. The `Service` provides `GetParents()` used by `GetInheritedScopes()`.\\n\\n### Resource Permissions Store (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/store.go`)\\n`flatResourcePermission.IsInherited(scope)` returns true for managed permissions whose scope does not directly match the requested resource (i.e., they come from a parent folder). This powers the display of inherited vs. direct permissions in the UI.\\n\\n### Folder/Dashboard Resource Permission Services (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/`)\\n`ProvideFolderPermissions()` and `ProvideDashboardPermissions()` both configure an `InheritedScopesSolver` callback that calls `GetInheritedScopes()`, wiring the inheritance mechanism into the resource permissions evaluation engine.\"\n}\n",
